 Do you know that by throwing green cabbage leaves in the trash you waste a very good source of calcium? Perhaps you will not know that the green leaves of cabbage which we throw during cleaning are very good medium of calcium
 gobhi kii pattiya main prachur maatra main calcium or aayran paaya jaataa he
 The amount of calcium in these leaves is not as much as any other vegetable
 saath hi isaki pattiyaan fibre kaa bhi acha sorce hoti hai
 While eating its leaves makes bones strong, digestion is good, while it is also very effective in increasing immunity
 gobhi kii 100 gram pattee se kareeb 600 milligram calcium praapt hota he
 There is a large section of our country which cannot afford milk and other dairy products
 aise logon ke liye calcium kii maatra kii purti karne kaa ye ek bahut sasta or acha rasta he
 It is also important to choose the right leaves: You should choose similar leaves of cabbage which are green, shiny and of good quality
 murajhaai hui or peelaapan lee hui pattiyon kaa istemaal na karen
 Wash the leaves thoroughly before use
 kaise karen istemaal?gobhi kii pattiyaan kranchi or halkaa swaad liye hue hoti hai
 However, if you want, you can mix and cook them in any other vegetable
 ise donon tarah se khaaya ja saktaa he
 You can cook it or eat it raw like a salad
 soup or duusare peya main bhi inhen upar se maheen katkar daalaa ja saktaa he
 If you want, then finely chop it and make parathas like spinach and fenugreek parathas
 ise salad ke taur par bhi istemaal kiya ja saktaa he
